  17              	;@"																			"
  18              	;@"*************************************************************************"
  19              	;@"                                                                         "
  20              	;@"       This code expands on my earlier SmartStart bootstub assembler for "
  21              	;@" the Pi3. It directly supports multicore operation in C/C++. To do that  "
  22              	;@" it provides stack space to each core and provides a modified bootloader " 
  23              	;@" spinlock that protects against registers X0-X7 trashed. As any C/C++    "
  24              	;@" 64 bit compiler will trash those registers, to use C/C++ in multicore   "
  25              	;@" programming this protection must be done.								"
  26              	;@"       This is a matching paired AARCH64 stub for the 64bit linker file  "
  27              	;@" and carries the samme arrangement as AARCH32 to ease porting.		    "
  28              	;@"																            "
  29              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"*/

  35 0000 0C000010 		adr x12, _start							// Hold boot address in high register R12
  36 0004 610D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_BootAddr					// Address of RPi_BootAddr

  40 0010 810D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_IO_Base_Addr				// Address of RPi_IO_Base_Addr

  42

  74 0060 840C0058 	    ldr x4, = __EL0_stack_core0				// Address of EL0_stack_core0 stack pointer value

  79 0074 630C0058 	    ldr x3, = __EL1_stack_core1				// Address of EL1_stack_core1 stack pointer value

 169 013c 1F4400B8 		str	wzr, [x0], 4
 170 0140 7F0000EB 		cmp	x3, x0
 171 0144 C8FFFF54 		bhi	.bss_zero_loop
 172              	.bss_cleared:
 173              	
 174              	//"================================================================"
 175              	//			Core0 will bring Core 1,2,3 to secondary spin 
 176              	//"================================================================"
 177              	#define spin_cpu1 0xe0
 178 0148 011C80D2 		mov x1, #spin_cpu1						// Spin core1 jump address
 179 014c 62080058 		ldr x2, =multicore_start				// Function we are going to call
 180 0150 220000F9 		str	x2, [x1]							// Store the function address to core1
 181 0154 9F2003D5 		sev										// Wake core1 up
 182 0158 83030058 	 	ldr x3, =RPi_CoresReady					// Set CoresReady count address
 183              	.WaitCore1ACK:
 184 015c 610040B9 		ldr	w1, [x3]							// Read CoresReady count
 185 0160 3F080071 		cmp	w1, #2								// Wait for setting of second core ready
 186 0164 C1FFFF54 		bne	.WaitCore1ACK						// Core1 not ready so read again
 187              	#define spin_cpu2 0xe8
 188 0168 011D80D2 		mov x1, #spin_cpu2						// Spin core2 jump address
 189 016c 62070058 		ldr x2, =multicore_start				// Function we are going to call
 190 0170 220000F9 		str	x2, [x1]							// Store the function address to core2
 191 0174 9F2003D5 		sev										// Wake core2 up
 192 0178 83020058 	 	ldr x3, =RPi_CoresReady					// Set CoresReady count address
 193              	.WaitCore2ACK:
 194 017c 610040B9 		ldr	w1, [x3]							// Read CoresReady count
 195 0180 3F0C0071 		cmp	w1, #3								// Wait for setting of third core ready
 196 0184 C1FFFF54 		bne	.WaitCore2ACK						// Core2 not ready so read again
 197              	#define spin_cpu3 0xf0
 198 0188 011E80D2 		mov x1, #spin_cpu3						// Spin core3 jump address
 199 018c 62060058 		ldr x2, =multicore_start				// Function we are going to call
 200 0190 220000F9 		str	x2, [x1]							// Store the function address to core3
 201 0194 9F2003D5 		sev										// Wake core3 up
 202 0198 83010058 	 	ldr x3, =RPi_CoresReady					// Set CoresReady count address
 203              	.WaitCore3ACK:
 204 019c 610040B9 		ldr	w1, [x3]							// Read CoresReady count
 205 01a0 3F100071 		cmp	w1, #4								// Wait for setting of third core ready
 206 01a4 C1FFFF54 		bne	.WaitCore3ACK						// Core3 not ready so read again
 207
